#================================== 
# IVS source Name Translation Table  
#================================== 
# File format      : 06-Nov-2014  
# Date last revised: 27-Jul-2017 
# 
# Columns      Format             Content 
# 
#   1 -   8    A8                 IVS source name 
#                                 Source name used now or in the past in IVS schedules and databases 
#  11 -  26    A16                J2000 source name long 
#                                 ICRF designations following the recommendations of the IAU Task Group on Designations 
#  29 -  38    A10                J2000 source name short 
#  41 -  48    A8                 IERS designations source name constructed from B1950 coordinates 
#  51 -  62    A12                JPL source name 
#  65 -  79    I2,1X,I2,1X,F9.6   Right ascension in J2000 
#  82 -  96    I3,1X,I2,1X,F8.5   Declination in J2000 
#  99 - 118    A20                Source of position information 
# 121 - 130    I4,-,I2,-,I2       First date 
# 133 - 172    A40                Alternate names 
# 
#  The token in a column "-" indicates that the source name is the same as the IVS name.
#  If an entry is blank we do not have information about the source name in this format.
# 
#--------------------------- 
# Construction of the table: 
#--------------------------- 
# IVS names of 6011 sources either in blokq (Calc/Solve) or manually added from private communication 
# J2000 names (long), IERS names, and coordinates from TN35 for the 3414 ICRF2 sources 
# Coordinates from latest GSFC catalog if exist for the other sources. If not, a priori coordinates from blokq. 
# First date from latest GSFC catalog or TN35 if earlier 
# J2000 names (short), missing IERS names, and alternate names from source.names (rfc catalog, L. Petrov) 
# JPL names from xka-tcov-140918.cat_iers (XKa catalog, C. Jacobs) 
# Missing J2000 names (short) from sources.vlba.2012jul (SCHED catalog) 
# Alternate names (V-C&V) from xka-649_cat (XKa catalog, C. Jacobs) 
#  
# Contact information: Karine Le Bail, NVI Inc - karine.lebail@nasa.gov 
# 
# Note: Source positions are included in this file in order to unambiguously identify the source. The source positions are good, but not definitive. 
# In general we take source positions from published data unless we believe these are wrong. For example, almost all ICRF2 source positions are taken from TN35. 
# However the inclusion of more recent data shows that a few of these positions are incorrect. In these cases we use alternate data sources for the position. 
#

# Total number of sources in the table: 6011
